As veterans and their families not be a victim of cybershachrai

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-07-12T12:00:00-04:00

Description: Kіberfront for the Vorog is not Mensh, Azhzh Garyak Battlefield. Behind the pre -nuclear of the omnipotent ... War with Ukraine 2022, the war with Ukraine Latest news today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, the war with Ukraine in 2022 will be or not, will there be war With Ukraine, in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['359537878_590744709904359_6139663621893418083_n.jpg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'КІБЕРБЕЗПЕКА', 'МІНВЕТЕРАНІВ']

Category: News

The cyberfront for the enemy is no less important than the hot field of battle. With the help of a world web, the aggressor tries to spread the Kremlin propaganda, mislead Ukrainians, provokes cooperation, blackmails and banies. In the war, criminal fraudsters, which are used by various schemes of mischief and illegal profit, were also intensified during the war. In particular, the famous form of "military school" - pseudogloders who allegedly raise funds for assistance of the Armed Forces, wounded defenders or their families. As well as phishing is one of the most common apartments, reportsMinistry of Veterans.

Villains mainly use phishing references in schemes with payments that are otherwise related to war, they create pages-clones that is fake. Scams for this purpose require, for example, to introduce personal data and a bank card number allegedly for funds for funds or providing a certain social service. Having received the necessary requisites, they assign money from other people's accounts.

Therefore, it is extremely important for the most citizens to adhere to the right clergygiene.

Meanwhile, the Ministry of Veterans of Ukraine reminds the veterans of their families about compliance with the rules of cybergigiene:

  • not to inform confidential information, including bank card data, to third parties; (To pay certain social services, the Ministry of Veterans of Ukraine uses only a personal account number of a veteran or a member of his family(IBAN)); * Do not go for the dubious hyperlinks that send you. (Note that official pages of state bodies, charitable organizations, banking structures in messengers and social networks should be verified(contain the mark); * to receive information, especially about financial payments from the Ministry of Veterans, only from official sources.* In case of fraudulent suspicion - immediately report to law enforcement agencies.

Remember that even in war conditions, real bank staff, or state -level workers do not ask for such information.

If you have been a victim of cyberchary or found fraudulent actions, you can turn on legal aid or advice:

Cyber Police Site: https://ticket.cyberPolice.gov.ua/or Cyber Police Department, calling 0 800 505 170 170, can be recorded on an e -mail callcentter@cyberPolice.gov.ua, you can also turn to the nearest police station.

You can get free legal aid at the free number 0 800213 103.

The enemy continues to focus the main efforts on Kupyansk, Lyman, Bakhmut, Avdiiv and Mariinsky directions, heavy fights continue. 29 combat clashes took place.

In the Marine direction, under the enemy fire of artillery, our defenders reflect the attacks in the areas of settlements of Pobeda, Novomikhailivka and Marinka. The erod fired at more than 15 settlements, including Konstantinovka, Marinka, Venta and Elizabetivka.

Ukraine and Germany have started systematic cooperation in the field of strategic communications

Description: The Berlinі is a Dodennaya Ukrainian-Imetskiy Semіnar at the sphere of strategic ... Images: ['64ad60c807bac057059615_730x360.jpeg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'МЗС УКРАЇНИ']

Category: News

In Berlin, a two-day Ukrainian-German seminar is held in sphereristical communications for the exchange of experience in the field of struggle of melting and the implementation of cultural diplomacy projects, [reports] reportsForeign Ministry of Ukraine.

The event was opened from Ukraine by the First Deputy Foreign Minister Eminzhaparov, who, in particular, noted that to fruitful Ukrainian-German work in political, economic, defense and humanitarian industry, cooperation is added in the direction of combating misinformation and strategic communications. According to her, you can overcome the challenges in the information sphere by only partners' efforts.

“Since 2014, Ukraine has developed a huge experience and has actually become one of the coarse leaders in the field of misinformation. We are ready to share the best practices with our partners, to study their experience and suggestions, to take coordinated steps to bring to foreign audiences about Russian aggression against Ukraine, to refute Russian fakes, to confront Russian propaganda and misinformation, ”Emminazharova stressed.

She spoke about successful examples of cooperation in the field of strategic communication with the countries of the Lublin Triangle, the United Kingdom and France, and listed the resonant information projects developed by the Foreign Ministry of Ukraine.

The first deputy minister paid special attention to the possible joint efforts of the deputy to counteract the impact of Russian misinformation in the countries of Africa, Asia Talatyn America. In particular, she informed the participants about the strategy of new horizons developed in the Ministry of Internal Affairs for the construction of proactive, pragmatic trial cooperation with African, Asian and Latin American Ukrainians.

Emine Dzhaparova also noted the importance of closing the Russian state -owned person, which is engaged in propaganda abroad, to maintain the stability of the stability with a staggering level and emphasized the readiness of the Ukrainian side to work with partners to achieve this goal.

Category: News

Illustrative photo

Prolonged Russian aggression in Ukraine has led to a great demand for medical people, in particular for rehabilitologists who will be engaged in the restoration of our warriors and civilian Ukrainians affected by full-scale and need physical and/or psychological rehabilitation, about it [reports] [reports] [reports] reportsGovernment portal.

The Government has approved a resolution "On a state order for the training of specialists, scientific, scientific-pedagogical and working personnel, on the promotion and retraining of personnel in 2023." The document will significantly increase the training of rehabilitation professionals and psychologists in higher education institutions.

“Every day our warriors protect us from the aggression of the country-terrorist. Every day, our citizens find themselves under sighting attacks. Unfortunately, the request for rehabilitation, both physical and psychological, is increasing. We need to consolidate efforts for our heroes to receive all the necessary assistance. And the questions of professionals who are directly assisted are one. Today, the government has taken another step towards the implementation of hero policies - increased state orders for the training of specialists in the rehabilitation of tap psychologists. These are the specialists that Ukraine need to provide the complexes of the necessary rehabilitation assistance to all those who need it, ”Viktor Lyashko reported.

This year in Ukraine the volume of the state order will be increased for 1005 mint physical therapists and ergotherapists and another 40 psychologists. There will be about state order at medical universities that are subordinate to momosis.

In particular, the state training order for training increased:

  • bachelors in the specialty 227 "Therapy and Rehabilitation" -(from 50 to 625 seats)to prepare assistants of physical therapists and assistants of ergotherapists; * Masters in the specialties: * 227 "Therapy and Rehabilitation"(from 60 to 490 seats)for the preparation of physical therapists and ergotherapists; * 225 "Medical Psychology"(40 to 80 seats)for the preparation of psychologists.

future rehabilitologists will be taught at 8 MOH universities: The resolution also provides for an increase in the state order by 600 places for higher education institutions, which are under the control of the Ministry of Education of INAUKE. By specialties:

  • 053 "Psychology"(from 755 to 855 people)for the preparation of psychologists; * 227 "Therapy and Rehabilitation"(from 460 to 760 people)to prepare assistants of physical therapists and assistants of ergotherapists; * 231 "Social Work"(from 796 to 996 people)to prepare social workers.

The duration of training in the above specialties is 4 years to maintain the bachelor's degree on the basis of complete general secondary education with the cutting "Psychology", "Therapy and rehabilitation", "Social work"; 2 years will study students to obtain a master's degree on the basis of degree bacalurus in the specialty "Therapy and rehabilitation"; 6 years continue to obtain a master's degree on the basis of complete general average education in the specialty "Medical Psychology".

It should be noted that the issue of training and training of Tapsychologists' rehabilitation professionals is now crucial for the state, as increasing the number of specialists in this area will help in the future effectively overlapping the challenges and providing the necessary medical assistance to the victims.

RecallOn the eve of Prime Minister Denis Shmigal at a government meeting with the heads of the Ministry of Health, the Ministry of Education and Science, the Ministry of Economy, the Ministry of Social Policy and the Ministry of Finance, instructed all the responsible ministry for the training of doctors in the specialty 222 "Medicine".

On July 11, 2023, the Cabinet of Ministers of Ukraine adopted a decision on the CMU Resolution No. 1275 of November 11, 2022 “Some Issues of Defense Procurement for the Period of the Legal Regime of the Military Stan”, which will soon be published.

In this decision, part of the Ministry of Defense's proposals in the interests of defense capabilities was supported, namely, justice was partially restored against Ukrainian suppliers of goods, works and services for defense needs. The sophisticated Ukrainian business will be equal in rights with a foreign business, as a defense department. This will ensure predictability, rhythm of supply and payment under contracts(contracts).

Про це йдеться уматеріаліon the official website of the Ministry of Defense of Ukraine.

In particular, the Cabinet of Ministers has determined that as part of the value(prices)goods, works and services to meet the needs of the security and defense sector(Supply reward)performer.

“Formally protecting the interests of Ukrainian business is not a responsibility of the Ministers Defense. But only formally. Because the stable work of Ukrainian state and private suppliers of weapons, equipment, ammunition, objects of support is the direct interest of the Armed Forces and other components of defense forces. By protecting Ukrainian business, we protect the interests of defense. This is overwhelming sovereignty, our margin of strength. We need more Ukrainian weapons. Therefore, the Ministry of Defense consistently advocates that the Ukrainian business is developing, increasing production capacity. We simplify administrative processes, created a special mechanism - the MOU accelerator to quickly conduct OVT developers with bureaucratic slums. Thanks to this, we already have a durable dynamics for UAV production, we are already fully provided by the Army of Army helmets, bulletproof vests, basic positions of real property. Therefore, I considered and consider the requirements of the State Judicial Service to actually put the interests of foreign producers higher than Ukrainian and deprive the Ukrainian business right to profit. There is no logic in this, it is directly intensified by the interests of defense and the norms of the current legislation, ” - said Defense Minister Alexei Reznikov.The requirements of the State Judicial Service, which are considered by the Ministry of Defense, are unambiguous and appealed in court, with respect to the recovery of the funds specified as a profit from the Ukrainian business that cooperated with the sector and safety from the beginning of the legal regime of martial law.

This creates the conditions for violation of the stable work of Ukrainian producers there is a negative impact on the needs of the Defense Forces of Ukraine.

“Unfortunately, government colleagues, including those whose direct duty is to protect the Ukrainian economy, have not supported the position of the Defense Ministry in part, which is being restored to the restoration of justice since the beginning of martial law. For example, the defendants are current contracts with the leaders of the Ukrainian OPC, which end in 20124-25. We have hundreds of current contracts with Ukrainian producers this year. How to be with them? How to be with those that have already been fulfilled? The possibility of double interpretation of norms and pressure on business. Mindobors with this approach does not agree, so we will continue to challenge the approval of the State Judicial Service to law enforcement in court, ” - said the Ministry of Ministry of Ukraine Alexei Reznikov.

In Ukraine allowed not to go to driving school to make a "theory" on driving license

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-13T-11:01:45+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T19:01:45+03:00

Description: The Verkhovna Rada adopted a law on the introduction of administrative liability in the field of preparation and admission of drivers to drive vehicles. Ukrainians were also allowed to prepare for driving exams on "theory". - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16002...']

Tags: ['Автомобіль', 'Водійські права', 'Закон Савченко', 'Боротьба з корупцією', 'Верховна Рада']

Type: Article

The Verkhovnarad adopted a law on the introduction of administrative liability of the compliance of preparation and admission of drivers to driver.

Yaroslav Zheleznya, a MP from the Voice Parliamentary faction, was reported in telegram, reports Ukrinform.

He said that 271 MPs supported the legislative initiative.

The purpose of the law( №7354 )There are introduction of administrative and tort of reasons for bringing to the administrative responsibility of officials of preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers of vehicles of vehicles, in particular the territorial service centers of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, during the conduct of state accreditation of such institutions(Autoshkil), certification of their specialists and admission of persons to driving vehicles(Adoption of theoretical and practical exams, registration or issuance of a driver's license).

Читайте також: Стартував пілотний проєкт із забезпечення прозорихіспитів у сервісних центрах МВС It is noted that the main task of the law is to improve the state control of the sphere of preparation and admission of drivers to driving vehicles, reducing accidents on roads, reducing corruption risks during the preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers, conducting state accreditation of institutions(Autoshkil), compilation of theoretical and practical exposures, etc.

The Law of Ukraine on Administrative Offenses is supplemented by Articles 127(3), which establishes the administrative responsibility of the power of preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers and 127(4), which establishes administrative responsibility for violation of the procedure of state accreditation of establishments that carry out training, retraining and advanced training of drivers of transport equipment, certification of their specialists and the procedure for passing the examination for obtaining the right to drive vehicles or issuance of a certificate.In addition, changes are made to Articles 221, 222 and 255 of the Code of Administrative Offenses in order to regulate the issue of administrative liability by overwhelming articles.

Amendments to Article 15 of the Law of Ukraine "On Traffic" are proposed to be implemented for a person who wants to obtain the right to manage transport equipment of the relevant category or type, the ability to carry out self -preparation in a standard curriculum. That is, the person will have a choice, to contact special institutions(Autoshkil)Or master the content of the theoretical module of a typical curriculum yourself.

The adopted law is expected to facilitate more effective implementation of control functions Ministry of Internal Affairsin the field of preparation and admission to drivers of vehicles. As reportedEarlier, the Interior Minister Igor Klimenko announced a decrease in the number of existing centers from 148 to 55 in order to minimize corruption during the driving license.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-13T-4:35:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T21:35:00+03:00

Description: There can be no experiments on the replacement of compulsory Ukrainian dubs of foreign films with titration. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16104...']

Tags: ['Кіно', 'Українська мова', 'Англійська мова', 'Кремінь', 'Мовний омбудсмен', 'Дубляж']

Type: Article

There can be no experiments on the replacement of compulsory Ukrainian dubs of foreign films.

According to Ukrinform, the Ombudsman Taras Kremin emphasized this, reports press service Commissioner.

“There can be no experiments on cinema and replacement of Ukrainian dub -foreign films with titration!Citizens of Ukraine do not oblige to leave any other language other than the state, ”Kremin said.

He noted that the current legislation did not prohibit the broadcast of films with non -state language in the range of up to 10%.

*!(https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-culture/3730910-gorovij-vvazae-so-pokaz-filmiv-anglijskou-z-ukrainskimi-subtitrami-znisit-kinoteatri.html)“One of the cinemas in the center of the capital conducted such experiments and invited to watch foreign films without dub. However, such sessions were not used, because, on the one hand, there is insufficient level of proficiency in other languages, and on the other, Ukrainian dub is the most interesting, the most delicious, I would say so, ”the Language Ombudsman said.

The Commissioner also added that in order to study English in Ukraine, other ways need to be found, starting with increasing the level of English language skills, and education applicants, and those categories of citizens for which English is a mandatory requirement.

As reported by Ukrinform, on June 28, the President of Ukraine Vladimir Zelensky struckIn the Verkhovna Rada, the bill “On the use of English spoke to Ukraine”(№9432).

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Images: ['630_360_16104...']

Tags: ['Медицина', 'МОЗ', 'Законопроєкт', 'Канабіс']

Type: Article

The health care of Ukraine assures that the use of medicines by the use of medical cannabis will be strictly monitored.

According to Ukrinform, the ministry reported on Facebook.

У МОЗ заявили, що Україна зробила важливий крок до спрощення доступу до ліківна основі медичного канабісу. Верховна Рада 268 голосами ухвалила у першомучитанні урядовий законопроєкт № 7457.

«Дякуємо всім народним депутатам за їхні голоси та громадськості – запідтримку цієї дуже корисної ініціативи. Це був наш спільний тест нагуманність, і ми успішно його склали!» - зазначили у МОЗ.

В міністерстві підкреслили, що про потрапляння у вільний обіг препаратів звмістом медичного канабісу не йдеться. «Застосування ліків буде жорсткоконтролюватися, як це вже відбувається з наркотичними препаратами», -наголосили в МОЗ.

“It can be stated that we are in the summer peak of consumption that has increased precisely. Even the time of peak hours has changed, in particular, now, in fact, the peaks begin from the 16th and last somewhere to the 21st, to the 22nd. And the nashaenergosystem walks around the edge. Consumption is still possible to cover, but it is very difficult to use, ”Kharchenko said.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

The former chief engineer of Chornobyl AAZ, expirer of the Minister of Fuel and Energy said this in a comment to Ukrinform.(2002-2006)Nicholas Steinberg.

«Sale of nuclear equipment and accessories to other countries an epidemic of special export control. This means that BulgariaShe has transferred it to Ukraine, the permission of direct producers, that is, Russia. Accordingly, the Tripartite Agreement should be signed: Russia-Bolgaria-Ukraine. According to the agreement, the author assumes the responsibility and obligation to use the use of nuclear equipment, which is the object of dual -purpose. Such conditions are envisaged by the system of international law in order to prevent the distribution of nuclear weapons and are under the control of the IAEA, ” - said Shchetinberg.

According to him, before buying the mentioned nuclear equipment in Bulgaria it is necessary to carry out its technical analysis, since unused reactors have been more than 20 years old.

In addition, this possible purchase of nuclear reactors of Russian production of the state -made production will cost Ukraine, since these installations do not have a whole recruiting equipment that is nowhere in the world, except Russia, is unprepared as it is Soviet development.In addition, the expert has a great doubt that the American company Westinghouse can be engaged in the installation of nuclear installation of Russian development, despite the fact that the Ukrainians themselves have the greatest experience of building nuclear blocks of this project in China, Iran, India.

The Council plans to introduce electronic agrarian receipts in Ukraine

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-13T16:36:25+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T16:36:25+03:00

Description: At a meeting on July 13, 2023, the Verkhovna Rada approved the bill "On Electronic Agrarian Receipts" (No. 9266), which introduces a new financial instrument for lending agricultural production in Ukraine. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_15686...']

Tags: ['Кредит', 'Верховна Рада', 'Аграрії']

Type: Article

The Verkhovna Rada at the meeting on July 13, 2023 approved as the basis of the draft law "Proelectronic Agrarian receipts"(№9266), which introduces a new financial tool for lending agricultural production in Ukraine.

According to Ukrinform, the first deputy chairman of the Verkhovna Rada Committee of Questions of Finance, Tax and Customs Policy Yaroslav Zheleznyak reported in telegram.He noted that the bill was supported by 270 people's deputies.

According to the text Explanatory Note, documentary electronic agrarian receipts as non -emission securities by velectronic form. In this case, the document does not abolish the actions of the Law on Agrarian Settlements, but introduces a new financial instrument of lending, along with traditional, paper receipts.

Read also: in the NBU Council declare no threats for a volatile banking systemThe bill stipulates that an electronic agrarian receipt is a state-wide object of circulation in the capital markets and will be able to be the object of sale and a source of profit. Electronic agrarian receipts will exist an electronic document in the register of electronic agricultural receipts.

The document expands the range of entities that can issue electronic agricultural records, at the expense of agricultural cooperatives, as well as simplify the order of issuance, circulation and termination of electronic agrarian receipt comparative paper.

Read also: new marketing year for agrarians in: "old" problems and risks increasingAt the same time, the bill is expanding compared to traditional paper agrarian disclosures. Yes, the subject of collateral can be: abdomen and products of animal origin, products of their primary processing, as well as the harvest.

It is envisaged that the accounting of the rights to electronic agrarian receipts and rights with electronic agrarian receipts will be carried out in the system of depository securities, and the circulation of such receipts - only in the depository system of Ukraine.

Type: Article

There will obviously no new significant wave of Ukrainians abroad in Ukraine.

PTUKH NAS of Ukraine, Candidate of Economic Science Poznyak during a panel discussion on the topic: "Is there hope to return all the Ukrainians home?" In the Media Center Ukraine - Ukrinform.

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T17:56:36+03:00

Images: ['630_360_15369...']

Tags: ['Мінфін', 'Сергій Марченко', 'Відновлення України']

Type: Article

In the first month of 2023, Ukraine was able to mobilize the necessary international support for macro -financial stability, and only $ 3.87 billion was obtained for a quick renewal.

According to Ukrinform, this was reported Ministry of Finance of UkraineFollowing the meeting of Minister Sergey Marchenko with a special President of France on assistance and restoration of Ukraine Pierre Elbron.

The meeting took place on July 13, the ministry noted. The parties to discuss the Library of the Mechanism of the Coordination Platform of Donors of Ukraine, the need for fast -renewal, as well as the issue of preparation and implementation of financial tools for Ukraine(Ukraine Facility)from the EU.

During the discussion of the activities of the donor coordination platform, the Ukrainian Minister noted that during the first months of 2023, the main efforts were focused on ensuring the projected and rhythmic budget support, as well as financing the restoration of Ukraine.

“In general, we have a commitment to donors to give up to $ 42.5 billion. In 2023, in 2023, to finance the deficit of the State Budget of Ukraine. Thanks to the coordinated work of the Government of Ukraine with international partners, the current work of the platform is focused on the further detailing of the priority needs of restoration, the current state of payments and the capacity of the projects at the stage of early reconstruction, ”Marchenko detailed.

At the same time, he noted that there is some discrepancy between the projects that partners want to intensify and our needs. That is why the Ukrainian side and international donors now coordinate the list of urgent projects for the restoration of tannial resources.

Of all the financial obligations of partners for the restoration of Ukraine, there are only 3.87 billion. The United States meets the needs of a rapid recovery, which is estimated at $ 14.1ld. USA. At the same time, as the minister emphasized, a rapid recovery is a tin priority because it helps to create safe living conditions for Ukrainian, as well as the economic restoration of the country.The Minister of Finance reminded that during the Conference on Recovery of Ukraine(URC-2023), which took place at the end of June in London, EU leaders announced the formation of a new financial instrument for Ukraine(Ukraine Facility). Цейінструмент стане частиною багаторічної фінансової програми ЄС на 2024 - 2027роки. Ukraine Facility буде зосереджено на підтримці макрофінансовоїстабільності України, сприянні відновленню, відбудові та модернізації, а такожсприятиме переходу до "зеленої", цифрової та інклюзивної економіки.

За словами Марченка, новий Фінансовий інструмент для України буде містити триосновні компоненти: фінансову підтримку у вигляді безповоротної та кредитноїпідтримки України; інвестиційну рамку, призначену для залучення приватних тадержавних інвестицій; технічну допомогу та допоміжні заходи, включаючиекспертну допомогу з питань реформ.

“Для імплементації механізму Ukraine Facility уряд України має розробити Планз відновлення, реконструкції та модернізації. Цей План буде орієнтиром і дляінших програм допомоги донорів України”, - підсумував міністр.

Military assistance to Ukraine has a positive effect on the economies of partner countries-lush

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-13T18:16:56+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T18:16:56+03:00

Description: The head of the National Bank Andriy Pyshny believes that military assistance to Ukraine has a positive impact on the economies of our partners. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16651...']

Tags: ['Економіка', 'допомога', 'Андрій Пишний']

Type: Article

The main bank Andriy Pyshny believes that military assistance to Ukraine has a positive impact on the economies of our partners.

He wrote about it in a column for Forbes Ukraine, reports Ukrinform.

"Since the beginning of a full -scale invasion of military assistance to Ukraine, 32 countries have been provided. Some of them in the amount of 0.5-1.0% of their GDP 2022. General in this direction before Ukraine during 2022 reached more than 60 billion US the world economy, "the NBU head.

We do not stop thank all our partners for large -scale support; The grounds of the lush, "it is really striking and decisive for winning."

At the same time, there are 5 reasons for Ukraine's international military assistance as economic losses of donor countries.

The first factor is the economic effect of dominoes, that is, we have a positive influence of partners' costs related to military assistance to Ukraine.

"Each currency spent in the defense sector has the potential to generate additional GDP through various channels. According to the NBU specialists, the increase in military expenses of donor countries by $ 1 is associated with an increase in IVPP by 0.65 during a year NBU Chairman.

At the same time, the most significant additional impact on the increase in the cost of defense will be over time-in one or two years after assistance, and reaching 0,79-0.87 USD.

"However, this is not all, because the positive effects will be maintained even in five years after spending," the lush adds.

Secondly, providing military assistance stimulates research and development in donor countries, and "it will contribute to long-term growth of productivity."

In addition, it is "mistakenly underestimating the possibility of testing weapons" and expanding opportunities for exporting weapons and finding new markets, which is where former Russian weapons were also at the expense of former buyers. These are the third and fourth processors.

Read also: lush in London received the Central Bankingawards Award

Fifth, according to the head of the NBU, "military assistance to Ukraine is a contribution of a new structure of global security." And in this context, he is convinced, assisting Ukraine with weapons and finances to achieve peace- it is an opportunity to reduce the overall expenditure in the future.

"So, we have the following conclusion: international assistance to Ukraine is a much smaller burden for the economy of partners than it is declared in those speculative ones that we are increasingly hearing," Lusny summed up.

"The first group of dozens of pilots who will go to study abroad, will be azhetov. There will be a second wave and so on-the first will already apply the weapons in the sky, the rest of the pilotivo the surrounding brothers in the flight line, "he said.

Poland, Romania, the Netherlands, the United Kingdom, Denmark and other partner countries-each of them, according to Ignati, will provide us with their sites and material for training in our aviation specialists.

Ignata told that in recent years, to the large -scale invasion of the eatery, future Ukrainian military pilots, that is, cadets of the flight faculty of Kharkiv University of Air Force, at the graduation of the Fifth COURSE have undergone flight practices in the battle parts for a long time. There is no such opportunity at this time, so the initial and basic preparation can be carried out in different partner countries, and this will, of course, will be a long process than retraining combat pilots on the F-16.

According to him, in the future our cadets can be prepared and abroad. Initially, on light -motor aircraft, but - the aircraft of the western, meaningful cabin is adaptive, as close as possible to the cabin of the Western fighter. It will continue to study on a jet aircraft, and then - non -indirectly on the fighter itself. For them, the main thing will be to understand the philosophy of Western aircraft after aircraft production and, of course, to know English for successful transaction. With this, according to Ignati, there are no problems, and even before going abroad, our aircraft is intensely prepared, improving their level of fertilization in a foreign language and studying the technique in the process of training.

Description: At the meeting, the Federal Government of Germany approved the first comprehensive strategy for China, which, among other things, called Beijing to a clearer position on Russian aggression against Ukraine and warned against the transfer of weapons of the Russian Federation. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16838...']

Tags: ['Китай', 'Німеччина', 'Україна', 'Росія']

Type: Article

At the meeting, the Federal Government of Germany approved the first comprehensive strategy of Ozkitai, in which, among other things, Beijing called for a clearer position against Russian aggression against Ukraine and warned against the transfer of weapons of the Russian Federation.

The 64-page document was published on the German Foreign Ministry website, some of his provisions were presented in Berlin by the head of the department Annalen Berbb, Ukrinform reports.

The "foreign policy" section of the document, in particular, refers to the relations of the PRC, which, especially after the start of a full -scale Russian aggressive warfare in front of Ukraine, "are of direct importance for the security policy of Germany."

“Russia's invaders against Ukraine is a fundamental violation of the statuon. China is unconvincingly protecting the sovereignty and territorial integrity of Ukraine, while supporting the anti -Natoto Russian narratives. We have a dialogue with China and urge him to clearly position ourselves with the anticipation of the anti -Russian invading war, ”the document goes.

It emphasizes that the permanent members of the UN Security Council have a special responsibility to comply and protect the UN Charter. Germany expects to support the sovereignty, territorial sake and principles of the UN Charter by "specific actions".

The closer cooperation between China and Russia in the field of weapons, including the supply of Chinese weapons in the context of Russian aggression, "had a direct impact" on the relations between China and EU and China and Germany, was warned in Berlin.

The German side reminded in this context that in a joint declaration of 4 February 2022, China and Russia pledged to significantly intensify the cooperation of the ear spheres and condemned the prospect of further expansion of NATO, claiming the ceiling spheres of influence in their respective regions.

The German government also warned Beijing from attempting to change the status quo in the Taiwanese prototon, which is central to the peace and stability of the Vasian Pichihooocian region and far beyond it.

Berlin is increasingly perceived by China as a "geopolitically important subject -safety policy", whose behavior also affects the interests of the safety of Europe, the document stated.

"For Germany, China remains a partner, a competitor, a systemic rival ... China has changed, which is why we should also change the way of working with China," the head of the foreign policy department has arranged during the presentation.“We want to work with ChinaSo we need China, but we also need China in Europe, ” - said Plomatka.

At the same time, on the basis of pandemic and war lessons in Ukraine, which demonstrated the dependence on Russian energy, Germany will try to diminish the dependence on the PRC, because "the more diverse trade chains, the more stable" is Germany.

Type: Article

Presidential Joe Biden confirmed that the Allies of Ukraine had agreed to guarantee security of Ukraine before its accession to the Alliance.

According to Ukrinform correspondent, he said this on Thursday during a trip to Finland at a joint press conference with the Finnish President Saulinini.

“We made it clear to the President Zelensky that we will not wait for the final decision to join NATOIn order to take an obligation to ensure the long -term security of Ukraine, ”he said.

He recalled that G7 leaders made a new joint declaration on Ukraine support. “I was glad to see the declaration immediately supported the northern countries(Europe)", He said, adding that any countries can join it" to negotiate bilateral security agreements with Ukraine, will officially become a member of NATO. "

Biden noted that NATO countries have confirmed "the unwavering support of Ukraine's Hrob derivative, which protects its country from cruel and inhumane attacks."

According to him, allies and partners of the US around the world understand that "it is not a struggle for the future of Ukraine, it is about sovereignty, safety of Isvododa as such."

"I want you to think of what happened if we did not do anything," he said.

The Allies also agreed to cancel the NATO Membership Action Plan, which is usually necessary for joining, "and simply created the way to membership for Ukraine," he noted, noting Kyiv's progress on the path of democratic transactions.

Biden once again stressed that no country could join NATO if war is going, otherwise NATO would also be at war.

Images: ['630_360_15686...']

Tags: ['Санкції', 'Верховна Рада']

Type: Article

The Verkhovnarad adopted a law on amendments to some legislative acts of Ukraine for the application of sanctions.

Yaroslav Zheleznya, a MP from the Voice Parliamentary faction, was reported in telegram, reports Ukrinform.

He specified that the initiative was supported by 314 people's deputies.

The law is aimed at improving the procedure for recovering the assets of individuals in the state income in accordance with the law, ensuring a proper consideration by the Supreme Anti -Corruption Court of cases on the application of sanctions.

It is envisaged to establish the State Register of sanctions in order to provide public access to up -to -date and reliable information about all entities for which personal sanctions are applied.

It is noted that the register is planned to place grounds for application, change or cancellation of sanctions, list sanctionsThe list of persons applied to each person applied to each person and information for grafting.

At the same time, the register will contain information on the bodies responsible for the implementation of the NSDC on the application of sanctions and information on the subject of the proposal on the application of sanctions.

It is envisaged that the NSDC apparatus shall ensure that the registry is created and operated, as well as not later than six months from the date of entry into force of the law, as well as to work on the beginning of its functioning in the Voice of Ukraine newspaper.

In addition, the law stipulates that the case of the use of sanction in the revenue of the state of assets is resolved by the Board within the three judicial anti -corruption court for 30(Previously - 10)days from the date of receipt of the statement in court.

The law is expected to ensure the implementation by the state in the face of effective sanction policy.

The Verkhovnarad adopted a law on the introduction of administrative liability of the compliance of preparation and admission of drivers to driver.

Yaroslav Zheleznya, a MP from the Voice Parliamentary faction, was reported in telegram, reports Ukrinform.

He said that 271 MPs supported the legislative initiative.

The purpose of the law( №7354 )There are introduction of administrative and tort of reasons for bringing to the administrative responsibility of officials of preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers of vehicles of vehicles, in particular the territorial service centers of the Ministry of Internal Affairs, during the conduct of state accreditation of such institutions(Autoshkil), certification of their specialists and admission of persons to driving vehicles(Adoption of theoretical and practical exams, registration or issuance of a driver's license).

Читайте також: Стартував пілотний проєкт із забезпечення прозорихіспитів у сервісних центрах МВС It is noted that the main task of the law is to improve the state control of the sphere of preparation and admission of drivers to driving vehicles, reducing accidents on roads, reducing corruption risks during the preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers, conducting state accreditation of institutions(Autoshkil), compilation of theoretical and practical exposures, etc.

The Law of Ukraine on Administrative Offenses is supplemented by Articles 127(3), which establishes the administrative responsibility of the power of preparation, retraining and advanced training of drivers and 127(4), which establishes administrative responsibility for violation of the procedure of state accreditation of establishments that carry out training, retraining and advanced training of drivers of transport equipment, certification of their specialists and the procedure for passing the examination for obtaining the right to drive vehicles or issuance of a certificate.In addition, changes are made to Articles 221, 222 and 255 of the Code of Administrative Offenses in order to regulate the issue of administrative liability by overwhelming articles.

Amendments to Article 15 of the Law of Ukraine "On Traffic" are proposed to be implemented for a person who wants to obtain the right to manage transport equipment of the relevant category or type, the ability to carry out self -preparation in a standard curriculum. That is, the person will have a choice, to contact special institutions(Autoshkil)Or master the content of the theoretical module of a typical curriculum yourself.

The adopted law is expected to facilitate more effective implementation of control functions Ministry of Internal Affairsin the field of preparation and admission to drivers of vehicles. France has approved a record defense budget that includes assistance to Ukraine

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-13T19:31:30+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-13T19:31:30+03:00

Description: On Thursday, July 13, the Parliament of France approved an increase in military expenditures caused by Russia's war in Ukraine and the rapid increase in global threats. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16813...']

Tags: ['Бюджет', 'Франція', 'Оборона', 'Україна']

Type: Article

On Thursday, July 13, parliamentiafranium approved an increase in military expenditures, which was initiated by Russia's war in Ukraine and the rapid increase in global threats.

As Ukrinform reports, it reports AP.

The new French defense budget for 2024 - 2030 will be 413 billion euros, which is more than a third exceeding the previous plan of military expenditures in 295 lLRD euros for 2019 - 2025.

The allocated money will allow the army to modernize the nuclear arsenal of France, increase intelligence costs and develop more weapons with remote control.

The adopted document also provides for doubling of military reservists and increased cyber defense, as well as an increase in weapons production capacity to assist Ukraine and for the proper provision of the French army.

The bill was finally approved by the National Assembly: the Lower Chamber of Wednesday 244 votes against 37, and a Senate - on Thursday 313 votes against 17.

According to the President FranceEmmanuel Macron, a large defense budget is necessary to ensure "our safety, our safety, our prosperity, our place in the world."

Images: ['630_360_14508...']

Tags: ['Євросоюз', 'Молдова', 'Україна', 'Залізниця']

Type: Article

European Commission and European Investment Bank(EIB)prepared recommendations for the priority steps to integrate the railway networks of Ukraine, Moldova Tajas; In particular, it is proposed to deploy a European track to Lviv and Chisinau.

About it reports Ministry of Community Development, Territories and Infrastructure of Ukraine, reports Ukrinform.

“On July 11, the European Commission and European Investment BankA study was published in which the deployment of the European track on the railway routes to Lviv of Chisinau. This will be the first step to improving the connection between Poland Tukraine, as well as between Romania and Moldova, ”the message reads.

According to the researchers, the priority steps of integration should be stated railway connection with Eurocolia(1435 mm)inter -circle/Katowice(Poland)and Lviv(Ukraine)as well as Yasami(Romania)Takishinevo(Moldova).

Що ж до розбудови української магістральної мережі залізниць стандарту 1435мм, їх пропонують розвивати за такими напрямками:

українсько-польський кордон (Medica/Mostyska)- Lviv;

Ukrainian-Polish border(Dorogusk)- Kovel - Sarnia - Korosten - Kiev;

Lviv - Krasne - Ternopil - Shepetivka - Zvyagel - Korosten;

Ukrainian -Slovak -Hungarian border - Chop - Uzhgorod - Sambir - Lviv;

Kyiv - Poltava - Krasnograd - Kharkiv/Dnipro;

Ukrainian-Polish border(Grebenne - Rava Ruska)- Lviv;

Lviv - Ivano -Frankivsk - Chernivtsi - Ukrainian -Romanian border(Bagrynivka);

Lviv - Ternopil - Khmelnitsky - Odesa - Dnipro - Zaporizhzhia - Mariupol.

At the same time, the study emphasizes that the introduction of new 1435 mm of corridors to Ukraine and Moldova is not enough to provide integration into the EU railway systems. For this purpose it is necessary to take additional measures, in particular, to harmonize the legislation in the field of railway transport with legal basis, to implement technical standards for operation of the network 1435 mm. Border and customs procedures are also simplified.

In addition to developing a 1435 mm railway network, existing 1520 mm should be upgraded(inclusive with the recovery of damaged as a result of war)In Ukraine, Poland and Slovakia, and with them depot, stations and sorting stations with reloading capacity, as well as internal intermodal -terminals and logistics centers.As reported, the Ministry of Restoration, JSC "Ukrzaliznytsia" and the European Bank of Reconstruction and Development begin the implementation of a project with a budget of 200 mln euro, which provides for the restoration, modernization of railway infrastructure for renewal of rolling stock.

The fire spread rapidly to the straw roof structures. In order to increase the volume of water supply to extinguishing, a special car was promptly involved to carry water from Kiev.

Rescuers of the 46th State Fire and Rescue Unit of SMT Kozin, 16-DPRC of Obukhiv, 17-DPRC Ukrainka, 64-DPRC village were involved in extinguishing. Vita Postiv, 29-DPRC Vasylkiv, 47th State Fire and Rescue Post of Glevakha town, 44-DPRC Chabana and fire and rescue units from Kyiv.

The Russian company tried to sell more than 10 thousand car parts of the production of the GAZ concern in the Ukrainian market. According to preliminary data, their value will set more than 3 million UAH. State Bureau of Investigation(DBR)Prevention of these auto parts in Ukraine and transferred them to the needs of defense.

About it reports DBRTo bypass the sanctions, representatives of the aggressor country planned to put smuggling products through third countries. According to the scheme developed by the scheme, the product was originally issued to Belarusian laid firms, and further sent to European companies, which already allegedly exported products to Ukraine.

Law enforcement officers exposed the equipment during an attempt to register the goods on the Kiev Mitnitsa. The recipient of the funds is a commercial structure whose bank account is open in the aggressor country.

The goods of the Russian manufacturer were removed as a result of criminal proceedings with a fundamental assistance to the aggressor country.

Утім, відмінні бачення все ж вдалосьпривести до спільного знаменника.

- As a result, we have what can be called uncertain certainty. They were certainly certain that Ukraine would become a member of NATO. They were a certain certainty that we will have to do it without a MAP, which is accepted as a positive fact. But the uncertainty remained in the case when the ceiling is, and in what specific steps Ukraine should take in order to happen, - he emphasized.

According to the expert, the decision to cancel the NATO membership plan in the NATO is positive and negative. The replacement of the MAC will be programs that will be evaluated by the Minister of Defense of Ukraine and the Ministers of Defense of the North Atlantic Alliance. Ukraine has been participating in such programs since 2003, that is, our country has been implementing the Donato Affiliation Program for 20 years.

  • Now you need an understanding of how the reforms will be implemented and which will be given to these resources. Because what reforms need to be implemented is a fact, but is usually not only a labor -intensive but also quite expensive process, - said.

Therefore, if the new program provides for the financing of technical expert assistance, it will be a big plus for Ukraine.

A recruitment is ongoing to participate in the experimental project to introduce a veteran assistant.

About it reportsMinistry of Reintegration of the Occupied Territories of Ukraine.

It is designed for veterans and members of their families, who are ready to help other veterans go through the transition from military service to civilian life, to obtain services and benefits that are guaranteed by the state.

War veterans and their families, victims of the Revolution of Dignity, etc. may take part in the project.

The application for participation can be submitted on the platform e-veteran.The selected participants will be sent for training, advanced training and work in one of the territorial communities in Vinnytsia, Dnipropetrovsk, Lviv or Mykolaiv regions.

During live broadcast in Telelorphone «Єдині новини»заступник командувача Східного угруповання військ Збройних Сил України зістратегічних комунікацій полковник Сергій Череватий розповів про обстановку насході України та, зокрема, в районі міста Бахмут.

— Наші війська мають частковий успіх на південному фланзі, закріплюються нарубежах, — розповідає офіцер. — Загалом ініціатива належить Силам оборони.Триває щоденна бойова робота. Під час п’яти бойовихзіткнень на цьому напрямку було знищено 71 окупанта, 141 — зазнав поранень іодин потрапив у полон. Підбито чотири ворожі танки, бойову машину десанту, двіустановки РСЗВ БМ-21 «Град», три гармати, дві САУ «Гіацинт-С», двапротитанкові ракетні комплекси, один зенітний ракетний комплекс «Стріла-10»,комплекс візуального спостереження «Муром-М» та п’ять БПЛА.

На Лимано-Куп’янському напрямку противник накопичує досить потужне угрупованняз повітрянодесантних та піхотних підрозділів, а також для підсиленняконцентрує підрозділи так званого бойового армійського резерву БАРС,територіальні війська, невеликі приватні військові компанії на кшталт«ветеранів» та штурмові роти «шторм-z», укомплектовані засудженими.

Як говорить полковник Сергій Череватий, цей напрямок залишається лідером закількістю артилерійських та авіаційних ударів ворога: тут противник обстрілявпозиції Сил оборони 665 разів та завдав 11 авіаударів. Також на цьому відтинкуфронту відбулось три штурми наших позицій — два біля Новоселівського і одинпоблизу Білогорівки. Усі спроби штурмових дій ворога були відбиті й він зазнавутрат: 28 окупантів знищено, 120 поранено. Також українські захисникиутилізували дві ворожі бойові машини піхоти, 240-мм самохідний міномет«Тюльпан», дві САУ «Акація», гаубицю Д-30, п’ять БПЛА, один дрон-камікадзе,один польовий склад з боєприпасами та сім автомобілів, що підвозили цібоєприпаси.

— Відбуваються бої, ворог неодноразово намагався прорвати нашу оборону, алевсі ці спроби виявилися невдалими, — свідчить Сергій Череватий. — Ситуаціяповністю контрольована.

На цьому закцентувала увагу старший аналітик фонду «Повернись живим» МаріяКучеренко під час дискусійної панелі на тему «Підсумки та оцінки Вільнюськогосаміту НАТО» у Military Media Center. Вонанаголосила, що від ситуації небажання дратувати путіна розширенням НАТО наСхід Альянс прийшов до чіткого твердження про те, що Україна неминуче маєстати членом Північноатлантичного Союзу.

Разом з тим експертка підкреслила, що ми дещо завищували очікування відсаміту, тому слід бути реалістами і розуміти, що взаємодія з партнерамипередбачає врахування насамперед їхніх безпекових інтересів. В цілому жпідсумки саміту можна вважати успішними для України.

— Ми побачили результат у вигляді коммюніке, ми побачили результат у виглядігарантій безпеки від Великої Сімки, — підкреслила вона. — Офіс Президента можетрактувати це як свій успіх. Документ, який готувався як Київський компакт ібув презентований як Київський компакт, ліг за основу тих гарантій, які намсьогодні запропонувала Велика Сімка.

Водночас до досягнутих результатів слід ставитись максимально прагматично,оскільки обіцянка членства у НАТО ще не є членством в Альянсі. Прийнятийдокумент містить певний ризик, оскільки передбачає можливість гальмуванняпроцесу вступу України до НАТО.

— У будь-який момент ми можемо повернутися до ситуації, коли нам говорять, щови не готові, ви маєте чудові гарантії, ми нормально спілкувались і не требафорсувати події, — зауважила Марія Кучеренко.

Тому необхідно розділяти емоційні очікування громадян України від результатівсаміту та критичний аналіз прийнятих у Вільнюсі рішень. Притаманне західнимпартнерам України безпекове бачення світу дещо відрізняється від загостреноговійною погляду з України, тож не слід очікувати, що держави члени НАТО будутьдіяти достоту точнісінько саме так, як хотілося б зараз українцям.

Про цеповідомляєСлужба безпеки України.

Зловмисником є кадровий співробітник управління фсб у Красноярському країІванченко Олександр Юрійович.

Встановлено, що він готував теракти проти Сил оборони і збирав інформацію ізприфронтових регіонів України. Робив це через декількох агентів, яких курувавособисто.

Так, у 2017 році Олександр Іванченко завербував киянина і після декількох«тестових» завдань «законсервував» його.

На початку повномасштабного вторгнення рф співробітник фсб «активував» свогоагента і дав йому вказівку прибути до Чернівецької області.

Там зрадник мав встановити і передати агресору локації залізничних вузлів ілогістичних складів, які задіяні для тимчасового базування і перекиданняукраїнських військ на фронт.

Розвідінформація потрібна була російським окупантам для здійснення серіївибухів на інфраструктурних об’єктах Буковини.

Втім, Служба безпеки спрацювала на випередження і затримала ворожого агента напочатку цього року.

The renewed housing legislation of Ukraine should take into account the needs of the highlights of accessible housing of war veterans and their families. After all, the number of persons of this category in the Russo-Ukrainian War by the deduction of members of the families of fallen defenders and defenders exceeds the memilion.

About it stressedFirst Deputy Minister for Veterans Affairs Alexander Pryhong during a public discussion "New Approaches to Housing Policy", which took place on the initiative of the Ministry of Community Development, Infrastructure of Ukraine(Ministry of Infrastructure).

Захід присвячено пошуку ефективного механізму забезпечення українськихгромадян доступним житлом, фінансуванню житлових програм, а також створеннюнової системи житлового законодавства. Участь у дискусії взяли представникипарламенту, офісу президента, міністерств і відомств, міжнародних організацій,органів регіональної і місцевої влади, громадських організацій.

Олександр Порхун зазначив, що за офіційними даними станом на квітень цьогороку на квартирному обліку в Україні перебувають понад 35 000 ветеранів війни.Зокрема, 29 017 осіб з числа ветеранів війни, які з 2014 року стали на захистдержави в період проведення антитерористичної операції, операції об`єднанихсил та заходів оборони, з них 1997 — особи з інвалідністю І-ІІ групи внаслідоквійни, 1015 — особи з інвалідністю ІІІ групи внаслідок війни, 488 — сім’їзагиблих (the dead)Defenders and defenders.

At the same time, more than 1 million people have been attracted to Ukraine with the beginning of a full -scale Russian invasion of Ukraine's native land. They will receive the status of a war veteran, in particular, a participant of combatants, with appropriate social guarantees, including in providing. Given the consequences of the war and the need for the reconstruction of the country, the financial resources of the state and local budgets will be restricted to provide guarantees, which are defined by the current Law "On the Status of War Veterans, Guarantees of Social Protection".

“Therefore, the system of social protection in the field of housing for veterans of war, their families need changes and new approaches. The state has to create the audience in which every citizen will be able to build a home, buy it or rent it, ”Alexander Pazhun emphasized.Among the short -term such can be available social lease of hostages or communal ownership, creation of social housing funds(Without the right to privatization), social support for war veterans by compensating for temporary accommodation costs(6 months and more).

На довгостроковий період потенційними рішеннями можуть стати державні гарантіїдля осіб з інвалідністю шляхом виплати грошової компенсації за житло, доступнаіпотека з компенсацією відсоткової ставки або першочергового внеску.

«Мінветеранів наразі працює над розробкою нового закону про основні засадидержавної ветеранської політики та впровадженням нових програм соціальноїпідтримки ветеранів війни та членів їх сімей. Зокрема, це компенсаціявідсоткової ставки за доступною іпотекою та компенсація витрат за тимчасовуоренду житла державної чи комунальної власності. Moldova reduces the tariff for transit of Ukrainian agricultural products in the direction of ports

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-14T01:19:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-14T01:19:00+03:00

Description: The Railway of the Republic of Moldova agreed to provide a discount on the transit transportation of Ukrainian agricultural products in the direction of ports of Reni, Dzhurguleshta and Galats. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16769...']

Tags: ['Експорт', 'Мінагро', 'Молдова', 'Порт', 'Україна', 'Зерно', 'Транзит']

Type: Article

The Moldova Railway Republic has agreed to provide a discount on the transit transportation of Ukrainian agricultural products in the direction of the ports of Reni, Dzhurjuleshta and Galats.

About it reports Ministry of Agrarian Policyand food of Ukraine, reports Ukrinform.

"The Moldovan railway has agreed to provide a discount of 27% of the existing tariffs for the transit transportation of Ukrainian agricultural products to the territory of the Republic of Moldova in the direction of ports of Reni, Dzhurguleshta and Galats," - it is reported.

New tariff conditions will be valid from July 15, 2023.

The Ministry of Agrarian Policy emphasizes that according to the new tariff conditions, the coefficient for discounts to basic tariffs is applied to compliance with the volume of transportation by all freight organizations.

Read also: Guterrash proposes Putin to continue " grain Vu agreement" in exchange for access to SWIFT Bank of the Russian Federation - ReutersThe tariff recalculation requires compliance with one of the two conditions: the performance of the installed volume of freight for a month and the average monthly volume of goods transferred over the last three months more or equal to the established volume of freight transportation per month.

As it was reported, in early June, Minister of Agrarian Policy and Food of Ukraine Mykola Solsky discussed with the Minister of Agriculture of the Taharical Industry of the Republic of Moldova Vladimir Pain Steps, will qualify the increase in the volume of transportation by the Moldovan railway Ukrainian agricultural products, including by lowering the tariff for them.

The connection has announced the allocation of an initial contribution of $ 100 million to finance the program in the agricultural sector, the implementation of which will start from Africa.

This is stated in the official statement of US Secretary of State Anthony Blinken, reports Ukrinform.

“We will never achieve food safety goals without fertile soils, and adapted and productive crops. The United States makes an initial hat of $ 100 million through the Prospects for Adapted Cultures and Soils(VACS)”, - said the head of the US Foreign Ministry.

He specified that VACS is part of a larger "feed the future" program(Feed the Future).
